const vacancyName = ()=> {
    var ff5 = document.querySelectorAll('.bloko-header-section-1 span')
    let vacancy = ''
    for (let i = 0; i < ff5.length; i++){
        vacancy = vacancy + ff5[i].innerHTML
    }
return vacancy
}
const companyName = ()=> {
    var company = ''
    var ff6 = document.querySelectorAll('.bloko-header-section-2.bloko-header-section-2_lite span')
    for (let i = 0; i < ff6.length; i++) {
        company += ff6[i].innerHTML
    }
return company
}
